Section 1:
1 HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES - FLOOR VERSION
2 STATE OF OKLAHOMA
3 2nd Session of the 60th Legislature (2026)
4 COMMITTEE SUBSTITUTE
FOR
5 HOUSE JOINT
RESOLUTION NO. 1069 By: Lawson of the House
6
and
7
Thompson of the Senate
8
9
10
11 COMMITTEE SUBSTITUTE
to refer to the people for their approval or
13 rejection proposed amendments to Sections 4 and 8 of
Article XVII of the Constitution of the State of
14 Oklahoma; modifying procedure for the Legislature to
create or alter counties and the equitable division
15 of assets and liabilities; providing updated legal
descriptions of counties; providing ballot title; and
16 directing filing.
17
18
19 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES AND THE SENATE
20 OF THE 2ND SESSION OF THE 60TH OKLAHOMA LEGISLATURE:
21 SECTION 1. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
22 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
23 the following proposed amendment to Section 4 of Article XVII of the
24 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
HJR1069 HFLR Page 1
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.
1 Section 4. The Legislature shall provide by general laws for
2 the creation of new counties or altering or changing lines and the
3 equitable division of assets and of liabilities, and the original
4 location of county seats in such new counties: Provided, That every
5 such question shall be submitted to the vote of the qualified
6 electors residing in the territory to be formed into such new county
7 or transferred to another county, and shall be approved by sixty per
8 centum of the votes cast in said election: Provided, That no new
9 county shall be formed of less than four hundred square miles
10 taxable area, nor with a population less than fifteen thousand
11 people, nor with taxable wealth less than two and one-half million
12 dollars, as shown by the current tax rolls. Nor shall any territory
13 be taken from an existing county for any purpose bringing the newly
14 created line of such existing county nearer than ten miles to the
15 county seat thereof. Nor shall the taxable area, population, or
16 taxable wealth of said existing county be reduced below that
17 required for a new county. Nor shall any territory, in any case, be
18 transferred from one county to an existing county, if, by such
19 transfer of territory, the county from which the territory be taken
20 will then be smaller in area than the county to which the addition
21 is made: Provided, That when territory is to be transferred from an
22 existing county to either a new or an existing county, there must be
23 sixty per centum of the vote cast in such particular territory in
24 favor of the transfer, and, in case the transfer be to an existing
HJR1069 HFLR Page 2
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.
1 coun ty, the acceptance of such territory must first be approved by a
2 majority vote of the electors of said county, at an election to be
3 called and held therefor, as may be provided by law. The limitation
4 as to area, valuation and population shall not be increased by the
5 Legislature.
6 SECTION 2. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
7 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
8 the following proposed amendment to Section 8 of Article XVII of the
9 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
10 Section 8. The State of Oklahoma is hereby divided into
11 Counties named and described as follows (all descriptions are
12 referred to the Indian Meridian and base line established by the
13 United States Geological Survey, 1895-1899; unless otherwise
14 specifically mentioned). Detailed Public Land Survey System (PLSS)
15 descriptions are referenced to the Bureau of Land Management (BLM)
16 New Mexico CADNSDI PLSS Township, First Division (Sections) and
17 Second Division (Section subdivisions and government lots)
18 Geographic Information System (GIS) vector digital data layers,
19 Version 2, published December 13, 2023:

12 SECTION 3. The Ballot Title for the proposed Constitutional
13 amendment as set forth in SECTIONS 1 and 2 of this resolution shall
14 be in the following form:
15 BALLOT TITLE
16 Legislative Referendum No. ____ State Question No. ____
17 THE GIST OF THE PROPOSITION IS AS FOLLOWS:
18 This measure amends the Oklahoma Constitution in Sections 4 and
19 8 of Article 17. This measure updates the provisions related
20 to the creation of new counties and changes to county
21 boundaries. This measure would still allow the Legislature to
22 pass general laws governing the creation of new counties,
23 changes to county lines, the fair division of county assets and
24 debts, and the original location of county seats. All other
HJR1069 HFLR Page 151
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.
1 requirements including voting requirements to form a county or
2 transfer territory and minimum requirements for land area,
3 population size, and taxable property value which are currently
4 listed in the Constitution would be stricken. These
5 requirements would still be governed by statutes passed by the
6 Legislature. This measure also provides updated legal
7 descriptions of all seventy-seven counties.
8 SHALL THE PROPOSAL BE APPROVED?
9 FOR THE PROPOSAL — YES _____________
10 AGAINST THE PROPOSAL — NO _____________
11 SECTION 4. The Chief Clerk of the House of Representatives,
12 immediately after the passage of this resolution, shall prepare and
13 file one copy thereof, including the Ballot Title set forth in
14 SECTION 3 hereof, with the Secretary of State and one copy with the
15 Attorney General.

As Amended and Coauthored.

11 COMMITTEE SUBSTITUTE
12 A Joint Resolution directing the Secretary of State
to refer to the people for their approval or
13 rejection proposed amendments to Sections 4 and 8 of
Article XVII of the Constitution of the State of
14 Oklahoma; modifying procedure for the Legislature to
create or alter counties and the equitable division
15 of assets and liabilities; providing updated legal
descriptions of counties; providing ballot title; and
16 directing filing.
17
18
19 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES AND THE SENATE
20 OF THE 2ND SESSION OF THE 60TH OKLAHOMA LEGISLATURE:
21 SECTION 1. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
22 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
23 the following proposed amendment to Section 4 of Article XVII of the
24 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
HJR1069 HFLR Page 1
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.

1 Section 4. The Legislature shall provide by general laws for
2 the creation of new counties or altering or changing lines and the
3 equitable division of assets and of liabilities, and the original
4 location of county seats in such new counties: Provided, That every
5 such question shall be submitted to the vote of the qualified
6 electors residing in the territory to be formed into such new county
7 or transferred to another county, and shall be approved by sixty per
8 centum of the votes cast in said election: Provided, That no new
9 county shall be formed of less than four hundred square miles
10 taxable area, nor with a population less than fifteen thousand
11 people, nor with taxable wealth less than two and one-half million
12 dollars, as shown by the current tax rolls. Nor shall any territory
13 be taken from an existing county for any purpose bringing the newly
14 created line of such existing county nearer than ten miles to the
15 county seat thereof. Nor shall the taxable area, population, or
16 taxable wealth of said existing county be reduced below that
17 required for a new county. Nor shall any territory, in any case, be
18 transferred from one county to an existing county, if, by such
19 transfer of territory, the county from which the territory be taken
20 will then be smaller in area than the county to which the addition
21 is made: Provided, That when territory is to be transferred from an
22 existing county to either a new or an existing county, there must be
23 sixty per centum of the vote cast in such particular territory in
24 favor of the transfer, and, in case the transfer be to an existing
HJR1069 HFLR Page 2
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.

1 coun ty, the acceptance of such territory must first be approved by a
2 majority vote of the electors of said county, at an election to be
3 called and held therefor, as may be provided by law. The limitation
4 as to area, valuation and population shall not be increased by the
5 Legislature.

11 Woodward is hereby designated the County Seat of Woodward County.
12 SECTION 3. The Ballot Title for the proposed Constitutional
13 amendment as set forth in SECTIONS 1 and 2 of this resolution shall
14 be in the following form:
15 BALLOT TITLE
16 Legislative Referendum No. ____ State Question No. ____
17 THE GIST OF THE PROPOSITION IS AS FOLLOWS:
18 This measure amends the Oklahoma Constitution in Sections 4 and
19 8 of Article 17. This measure updates the provisions related
20 to the creation of new counties and changes to county
21 boundaries. This measure would still allow the Legislature to
22 pass general laws governing the creation of new counties,
23 changes to county lines, the fair division of county assets and
24 debts, and the original location of county seats. All other
HJR1069 HFLR Page 151
BOLD FACE denotes Committee Amendments.

1 requirements including voting requirements to form a county or
2 transfer territory and minimum requirements for land area,
3 population size, and taxable property value which are currently
4 listed in the Constitution would be stricken. These
5 requirements would still be governed by statutes passed by the
6 Legislature. This measure also provides updated legal
7 descriptions of all seventy-seven counties.
8 SHALL THE PROPOSAL BE APPROVED?
9 FOR THE PROPOSAL — YES _____________
10 AGAINST THE PROPOSAL — NO _____________
11 SECTION 4. The Chief Clerk of the House of Representatives,
12 immediately after the passage of this resolution, shall prepare and
13 file one copy thereof, including the Ballot Title set forth in
14 SECTION 3 hereof, with the Secretary of State and one copy with the
15 Attorney General.
